'DI YANG NANG BSTAN GRUB MTHA' RIS MED KYI GSUNG RAB DAG DPAR DU
BSKRUN DANG BSKRUN 'GYUR GANG LA'ANG SBYAR CHOG PA'I DGE BSNGO'I
SMON TSIG TU SH'AKYA'I DGE SBYONG CHOS SMRA BA NGAG DBANG BLO
BZANG BSTAN 'DZIN RGYA MTSOS SBYAR BA'O,, ZHES SER SMAD GRVA
TSANG GI SNGAR SROL THUN MONG MA YIN PA'I TSOGS 'DON RNAMS SER

SMAD MKHAN PO KONG PO BYAMS PA DON YOD MCHOG DANG, DBU MDZAD
SMAR DKON MCHOG DPAL LDAN GNYIS NAS PHYOGS SGRIG ZHUS PA 'DI
BZHIN MKHAN RIN PO CHE MCHOG NAS JI LTAR BSKUL MA ZHUS PA BZHIN
AA RIR GNAS BZHUGS SER SMAD RGYAL RONG DGE BSHES BLO BZANG MTHAR
PHYIN LAGS NAS

PAR BSKRUN YON SBYOR GNANG SKABS LDI LIR BCA' BZHUGS SOG SPRUL
GU RU DE WA RIN PO CHE MCHOG NAS MTHUN 'GYUR ROGS RAM GNANG BA
LA BRTEN NAS 'JAM MGON RGYAL BA GNYIS PA'I BSTAN PA 'DI NYID
PHYOGS DUS KUN TU DAR RGYAS YUN DU GNAS PA'I RGYUR GYUR CIG, YI
GE PA NI DBU MDZAD
